$CATEGORY: $course$ / Examples / Do While Loops Counting1

::Do While Loops Level 1 #000::
How many times does the '*' print?
<pre>int g = 38;
do
\{
	cout << '*' << " ";
	g = g - 5;
\} while (g > 10);
</pre>	{
	=6
	~5
	~7
	~10
	~8
	}

<pre>int g = 41;
do
\{
	cout << '*' << " ";
	g = g - 5;
\} while (g > 21);
</pre>	{
	=4
	~3
	~5
	~6
	~0
	}
